local function createVM()
    local vm = {
        stack = {},
        memory = {},
        registers = {},
        pc = 1,
        
        opcodes = {
            LOAD = 1,   -- Load value to stack
            STORE = 2,  -- Store from stack to memory
            ADD = 3,    -- Addition
            SUB = 4,    -- Subtraction
            MUL = 5,    -- Multiplication
            DIV = 6,    -- Division
            JMP = 7,    -- Jump
            CALL = 8,   -- Function call
            RET = 9,    -- Return
            CMP = 10,   -- Compare
            XOR = 11,   -- Bitwise XOR
            AND = 12,   -- Bitwise AND
            OR = 13,    -- Bitwise OR
            NOT = 14,   -- Bitwise NOT
            ROL = 15,   -- Rotate left
            ROR = 16,   -- Rotate right
        },
        
        execute = function(self, bytecode)
            while self.pc <= #bytecode do
                local instr = bytecode[self.pc]
                local opcode = instr.op
                local args = instr.args
                
                if opcode == self.opcodes.LOAD then
                    table.insert(self.stack, args[1])
                elseif opcode == self.opcodes.STORE then
                    local val = table.remove(self.stack)
                    self.memory[args[1]] = val
                elseif opcode == self.opcodes.ADD then
                    local b = table.remove(self.stack)
                    local a = table.remove(self.stack)
                    table.insert(self.stack, a + b)
                -- Add more opcodes implementation
                end
                
                self.pc = self.pc + 1
            end
        end,
        
        reset = function(self)
            self.stack = {}
            self.memory = {}
            self.pc = 1
        end
    }
    return vm
end

local _vm = createVM()


local function initAdvancedSecurity()
    local security = {
        salt = '7265fae5d51a3f73a6b4dc7fc80664df50b4aed31d97d64e08b30d34d04cf8b8405f9f8509d1f49a2842af7c24070a194d3870550364ff70242b186a55e15bd3',
        keys = {"-nYp@~BY1G(z|`58#i)F[Ql{@KZ8&,i[ZZ{Iz4uuZ{_5]fzMWuH492RMm6F>4P+T", "jq}{i=32sDJ$B\]]ODl*dV8?='83.Xxm?L@m6gSu*'7.MF|X@kH$QVw`%b^VA>O"", "d$).Ohp|PfClAr'SU.#HJ,\IV*6rOu@'krP`2*x}wz1]WYH6M|"y"MP?/Hz*]nTx", "Y=1>wYL2}^awG=v24:bwU&B'<Q[msBB[yHRB0(S/qo6#YG9Rf3^by<2C\UjTl_7P", "=0Q`;_%:)<%(1P12J).jqmwBQb>"fn?D*\1mYncY@@pbB^EfkbWQvvIZl"XQ3t#-"},
        iterations = 1586,
        checks = 0,
        memory_regions = {},
        
        -- Advanced environment checking
        verifyEnvironment = function(self)
            -- Check for debugging
            if debug.getinfo or debug.getupvalue or debug.setupvalue or debug.sethook then
                return false
            end
            
            -- Check for modified environment
            if _VERSION ~= "Lua 5.1" and _VERSION ~= "Lua 5.2" and _VERSION ~= "Lua 5.3" then
                return false
            end
            
            -- Check for suspicious global modifications
            for k,v in pairs(_G) do
                if type(v) == "function" and debug.getinfo(v).source ~= "=[C]" then
                    return false
                end
            end
            
            -- Memory integrity check
            for region, hash in pairs(self.memory_regions) do
                if self:calculateHash(region) ~= hash then
                    return false
                end
            end
            
            return true
        end,
        
        -- Advanced decryption system
        decrypt = function(self, encrypted_text)
            local result = encrypted_text
            for i = #self.keys, 1, -1 do
                local key = self.keys[i]
                -- Reverse substitution
                local unsubstituted = ''
                for c in result:gmatch('.') do
                    unsubstituted = unsubstituted .. string.char((ord(c) - #key) % 0x110000)
                end
                
                -- Base85 decode
                local decoded = base64.b85decode(unsubstituted)
                
                -- XOR decrypt
                result = ''
                for j = 1, #decoded do
                    result = result .. string.char(bit32.bxor(decoded:byte(j), key:byte((j-1) % #key + 1)))
                end
            end
            return result
        end,
        
        -- Memory protection system
        protectMemory = function(self, region, data)
            local hash = self:calculateHash(data)
            self.memory_regions[region] = hash
            return data
        end,
        
        -- Advanced hashing
        calculateHash = function(self, data)
            local hash = 0
            for i = 1, #data do
                hash = (hash * 33 + data:byte(i)) % 0xFFFFFFFF
            end
            return hash
        end,
        
        -- Anti-tamper system
        validateCodeIntegrity = function(self, code)
            local expected_hash = '316f7f78b25b6f6d5e868dc911d5942086c78afa4e332511e5a1a95693b90f22'
            local actual_hash = self:calculateHash(code)
            return expected_hash == actual_hash
        end,
        
        -- Control flow protection
        obfuscateControlFlow = function(self, code)
            local parts = {}
            for line in code:gmatch("[^\n]+") do
                table.insert(parts, line)
            end
            
            local obfuscated = {}
            while #parts > 0 do
                local idx = math.random(1, #parts)
                table.insert(obfuscated, parts[idx])
                table.remove(parts, idx)
            end
            
            return table.concat(obfuscated, "\n")
        end
    }
    
    return security
end


local function executeSecureCode()
    local security = initAdvancedSecurity()
    local vm = createVM()
    
    -- Initialize protection systems
    local protected_env = setmetatable({
        -- Safe functions only
        print = print,
        type = type,
        tonumber = tonumber,
        tostring = tostring,
        select = select,
        unpack = unpack or table.unpack,
        -- Math functions
        math = {
            abs = math.abs,
            ceil = math.ceil,
            floor = math.floor,
            max = math.max,
            min = math.min,
            random = math.random,
            randomseed = math.randomseed,
        },
        -- String functions
        string = {
            byte = string.byte,
            char = string.char,
            format = string.format,
            len = string.len,
            lower = string.lower,
            upper = string.upper,
            sub = string.sub,
        },
        -- Table functions
        table = {
            insert = table.insert,
            remove = table.remove,
            sort = table.sort,
        },
    }, {
        __index = function(t, k)
            if security:verifyEnvironment() then
                return _G[k]
            end
            error('Security violation: Unauthorized access')
        end,
        __newindex = function()
            error('Security violation: Environment modification')
        end
    })

    -- Anti-debug hooks
    debug.sethook(function()
        if not security:verifyEnvironment() then
            error('Security violation: Debug detected')
        end
    end, "l", 1)

    local encrypted_code = m°}º¬µchah¡a©aªua¬£u¶ w½«¹²ª~tp¼µi~§«¯ky~¦e¦¹q¶a¬¹¶·°wtkºt§¸{a¯p°­¨p¶xm«©f¹m­³a}]==]
    
    -- Execution environment setup
    setfenv(1, protected_env)
    
    -- Memory protection
    security:protectMemory('code', encrypted_code)
    
    -- Integrity verification
    if not security:validateCodeIntegrity(encrypted_code) then
        error('Security violation: Code tampering detected')
    end
    
    -- Decrypt and execute
    local decrypted = security:decrypt(encrypted_code)
    local chunk = load(decrypted, 'protected_chunk', 't', protected_env)
    
    if chunk then
        return chunk()
    end
end

return (function()
    local success, result = pcall(executeSecureCode)
    if not success then
        error('Runtime security: ' .. tostring(result))
    end
    return result
end)()
